### Post by G_RAMAKRISHNAN on 2016-02-11
Hi

Last Month, I have bought dell laptop with Ubuntu 12.04 OS in built. 
I have install the CD driver lbp 2900 but no use system not accepting the printer driver.

It will very useful to me to solve this issue as soon as possible.

Regards
Ramakrishnan

---

### Post by Vladlenin5000 on 2016-02-11
What exactly have you installed from that CD, how and why? The "how" and "why" are asked because usually they come with drivers and software for Windows only...

The required drivers are here: [http://www.canon.co.uk/support/consumer_products/products/printers/laser/i-sensys_lbp2900.aspx?type=drivers&language=&os=LINUX](http://www.canon.co.uk/support/consumer_products/products/printers/laser/i-sensys_lbp2900.aspx?type=drivers&language=&os=LINUX)
Download & extract (right-click > extract here...)
Open the main folder,  then the 32-bit or the 64-bit folder according to your OS architecture, then "debian". You'll find two files inside.
Double-click each one and each will open with the Ubuntu Software Center, click the Install button and type your user's password when required.
